 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">September&nbsp;21, 2022 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GENERAL MILLS
REPORTS FISCAL 2023 FIRST-QUARTER RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AND RAISES FULL-YEAR OUTLOOK </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> were up 10&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

8&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of $1.35 increased 32&nbsp;percent from the prior year; adjusted diluted EPS
of $1.11 was up 13&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company raises full-year fiscal 2023 outlook </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 8 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS, Minn. &#150;
September&nbsp;21, 2022 &#150; General Mills (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for the first quarter ended August&nbsp;28, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We continue to deliver strong performance in a highly volatile operating environment,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief
Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;Given the strength of our first-quarter results and confidence in our ability to adapt to continued volatility ahead, we are increasing our full-year outlook for net sales, operating profit, and EPS
growth.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and standing for
good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures to further enhance
its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>First Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 4&nbsp;percent to $4.7&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 10&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower organic pound volume, including the impact of a voluntary recall on certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 450 basis points to 30.7&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs,
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, and the impact of market index pricing on bakery flour, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross
margin was up 20 basis points to 34.9&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation, the impact of market index pricing on
bakery flour, and supply chain deleverage. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $1.1&nbsp;billion was up 29&nbsp;percent, primarily driven by net gains on
divestitures, partially offset by lower gross profit dollars and unfavorable net corporate investment activity. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 23.0&nbsp;percent was up 440 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit increased
8&nbsp;percent, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin increased 70 basis points to 18.7&nbsp;percent.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> increased 31&nbsp;percent to $820&nbsp;million and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 32&nbsp;percent to $1.35, primarily reflecting higher operating profit. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.11 increased 13&nbsp;percent in constant currency, primarily driven by higher adjusted operating profit. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Notes on Comparability </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Financial results in the quarter reflected the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treat business in the first quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of the
European yogurt business in the third quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of certain international dough businesses in the third and fourth quarters of fiscal 2022; the acquisition of the TNT Crust foodservice business in the first quarter of
fiscal 2023; and the divestiture of the Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter results in fiscal 2023 also included the impact of a voluntary recall on certain international
<I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, which was a headwind to net sales and operating profit results in the International segment. Unallocated corporate items in the first quarter included an additional
$22&nbsp;million of charges related to product disposals associated with the ice cream recall that were excluded from adjusted operating profit results. Impacts of the recall are expected to be completed by the second quarter of fiscal 2023. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment increased 10&nbsp;percent to $3.0&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower pound volume and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from the Helper and Suddenly Salad divestiture. Organic net sales increased 12&nbsp;percent. Net sales increased
14&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks, 10&nbsp;percent in U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions, 9&nbsp;percent in U.S. Morning Foods, and 4&nbsp;percent in Canada. Segment operating profit of $778&nbsp;million was up 20&nbsp;percent as reported and in
constant currency, primarily driven by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation, lower volume, and supply chain deleverage. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for the Pet segment
increased 19&nbsp;percent to $580&nbsp;million, primarily driven by favorable net price realization and mix. Net sales results included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> benefit from the pet treats acquisition. Organic net sales were
up 14&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 7&nbsp;percent to $123&nbsp;million, primarily driven by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net
sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 21&nbsp;percent to $496&nbsp;million, primarily driven by favorable net price realization and mix, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17-point</FONT> benefit from market index
pricing on bakery flour. Net sales results also included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 18&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was down 25&nbsp;percent to
$54&nbsp;million, driven by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for the
International segment were down 30&nbsp;percent to $652&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume, including the impact of yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> headwind from
foreign currency exchange, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were down 2&nbsp;percent, driven by lower organic pound volume, including the impact of the ice cream recall, partially offset by positive
organic net price realization and mix. Segment operating profit of $35&nbsp;million was down 43&nbsp;percent as reported and down 34&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by lower volume, including the impacts of the yogurt and dough
divestitures and the ice cream recall, and higher input costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for
Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) increased 3&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by lower volume. Constant-currency net sales for
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ) were down 8&nbsp;percent, driven by lower volume. Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures totaled $20&nbsp;million compared to
$29&nbsp;million a year ago, primarily driven by higher input costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix at CPW. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other
Income Statement Items </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate items totaled $333&nbsp;million net expense in the first quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to
$56&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled
$107&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to $77&nbsp;million net expense last year, primarily driven by certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> favorable items a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded a net $431&nbsp;million gain on divestitures in the first quarter <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on
this item)</I>. Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled $2&nbsp;million of expense compared to a $4&nbsp;million net recovery a year ago <I>(please see Note 4 below for more information on these charges)</I>. Benefit plan <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income totaled $22&nbsp;million in the first quarter compared to $30&nbsp;million a year ago, primarily driven by an increase in interest cost, partially offset by lower amortization of losses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense totaled $88&nbsp;million in the first quarter compared to $96&nbsp;million a year ago, primarily driven by lower average
long-term debt balances. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 21.2&nbsp;percent compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 7 below for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was
19.7&nbsp;percent compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net earnings attributable to redeemable and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interests totaled $3&nbsp;million in the quarter compared to $11&nbsp;million a year ago, primarily driven by the sale of the company&#146;s interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and
Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl in fiscal 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities totaled $389&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2023 compared to $370&nbsp;million in the prior year, primarily
driven by higher net earnings, a favorable change in current assets and liabilities, and a favorable change in other operating items, partially offset by a net gain on divestitures. Capital investments totaled $91&nbsp;million compared to
$104&nbsp;million a year ago. Dividends paid increased 4&nbsp;percent to $325&nbsp;million. General Mills repurchased approximately 6.9&nbsp;million shares of common stock in the first quarter for a total of $501&nbsp;million compared to
$150&nbsp;million in share repurchases a year ago. Average diluted shares outstanding in the quarter decreased 1&nbsp;percent to 606&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2023 Outlook </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills continues to
expect the largest factors impacting its performance in fiscal 2023 will be the economic health of consumers, the inflationary cost environment, and the frequency and severity of disruptions in the supply chain. The company expects volume
elasticities will increase over the remaining quarters of fiscal 2023 but remain below historical levels. Relative to its initial full-year expectations, the company now expects lower volume elasticities and better volume performance, increased
input cost inflation to 14 to 15&nbsp;percent of total cost of goods sold, and increased investment in brand building and other growth-driving activities. Other key fiscal 2023 assumptions, including HMM cost savings of 3 to 4&nbsp;percent of cost
of goods sold, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-double-digit</FONT> positive price/mix, and an expectation for moderately lower supply chain disruptions, remain unchanged. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s updated full-year fiscal 2023 financial targets are summarized below: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Organic net sales</B> are now expected to increase 6 to 7&nbsp;percent, compared to the previous expectation
of 4 to 5&nbsp;percent growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

constant currency, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions and an estimated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from the ice cream recall. Adjusted operating
profit was previously expected to range between down 2&nbsp;percent and up 1&nbsp;percent in constant currency, including the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

currency, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions and an estimated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from the ice cream recall. Adjusted diluted EPS was
previously expected to range between flat and up 3&nbsp;percent in constant currency, including the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

reported net sales growth by approximately 4&nbsp;percent, and foreign currency exchange is still expected to reduce adjusted operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth by approximately 1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills will issue <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT> management remarks today, September&nbsp;21, 2022, at approximately 6:30 a.m.
Central time (7:30 a.m. Eastern time) and will hold a live, webcasted question and answer session beginning at 8:00 a.m. Central time (9:00 a.m. Eastern time). The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT> remarks and the webcast will be
made available at <U>www.generalmills.com/investors</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press release contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private
Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995 that are based on our current expectations and assumptions. These forward-looking statements, including the statements under the caption &#147;Fiscal 2023 Outlook,&#148; and statements made by
Mr.&nbsp;Harmening, are subject to certain risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from the potential results discussed in the forward-looking statements. In particular, our predictions about future net sales and
earnings could be affected by a variety of factors, including: the impact of the coronavirus <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(COVID-19)</FONT> pandemic on our business, suppliers, consumers, customers, and employees; disruptions or inefficiencies
in the supply chain, including any impact of the coronavirus <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(COVID-19)</FONT> pandemic; competitive dynamics in the consumer foods industry and the markets for our products, including new product introductions,
advertising activities, pricing actions, and promotional activities of our competitors; economic conditions, including changes in inflation rates, interest rates, tax rates, or the availability of capital; product development and innovation;
consumer acceptance of new products and product improvements; consumer reaction to pricing actions and changes in promotion levels; acquisitions or dispositions of businesses or assets; changes in capital structure; changes in the legal and
regulatory environment, including tax legislation, labeling and advertising regulations, and litigation; impairments in the carrying value of goodwill, other intangible assets, or other long-lived assets, or changes in the useful lives of other
intangible assets; changes in accounting </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we completed a new organization structure to streamline our global
operations. This global reorganization required us to reevaluate our operating segments. Under our new organization structure, our chief operating decision maker assesses performance and makes decisions about resources to be allocated to our
operating segments as follows: North America Retail; International; Pet; and North America Foodservice. We have restated our net sales by segment and segment operating profit amounts to reflect our new operating segments. These segment changes had
no effect on previously reported consolidated net sales, operating profit, net earnings attributable to General Mills, or earnings per share. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we acquired TNT Crust, a manufacturer of high-quality frozen pizza
crusts for regional and national pizza chains, foodservice distributors, and retail outlets, for a purchase price of $253&nbsp;million. We financed the transaction with U.S. commercial paper. We consolidated the TNT Crust business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $154&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the North America Foodservice segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. The
consolidated results of the TNT Crust business are reported in our North America Foodservice segment on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we completed the asset sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business to Eagle
Family Foods Group for $607&nbsp;million and recorded a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $442&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During
the first quarter of fiscal 2022, we acquired Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats
business into our Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $762&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I>, and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a
finite-lived customer relationship asset of $40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet segment and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(4)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we did not undertake any new restructuring actions. We recorded
$2&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the first quarter of fiscal 2023 and a $4&nbsp;million net recovery of restructuring charges in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 for previously announced restructuring actions. We expect these actions to
be completed by the end of fiscal 2024. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(5)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unallocated corporate expense totaled $333&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2023 compared to
$56&nbsp;million in the same period in fiscal 2022. In the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we recorded a $175&nbsp;million net increase in expense related to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories compared to a $24&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the same period last year. We
recorded $26&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in the first&nbsp;quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to $1&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments in
the first quarter of fiscal 2022. In the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we recorded a $22&nbsp;million charge related to a voluntary recall on certain international <I>H</I><I>&auml;</I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice
cream products. In addition, we recorded $2&nbsp;million of integration costs primarily related to our acquisition of TNT Crust in the first quarter of fiscal 2023 compared to $12&nbsp;million of integration costs related to our acquisition of Tyson
Foods&#146; pet treats business in the first quarter of fiscal 2022. Also, in the first quarter of fiscal 2022, we recorded a $21&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item, a $13&nbsp;million insurance recovery and $11&nbsp;million
of transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the first quarter of fiscal 2023 was 21.2&nbsp;percent compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent
for the first quarter of fiscal 2022. The 0.5 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits, partially offset by certain unfavorable tax components related to divestitures in the first quarter of fiscal
2023. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 19.7&nbsp;percent in the first quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see Note 8 below for a description of our use of
measures not defined by GAAP). The 2.0 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(8)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. We believe that these measures provide
useful information to investors, and include these measures in other communications to investors. For each of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences
between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to
investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in
addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our
consolidated net sales and segment net sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes.
We believe that organic net sales growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations,
acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales
growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are
presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at
the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year
results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide
useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2023 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted operating profit growth, adjusted diluted EPS growth, and free cash flow
conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions,
divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure without
unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates or the timing of acquisitions and divestitures throughout fiscal 2023. The unavailable
information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2023 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2023, we currently expect: foreign
currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and completed acquisitions and divestitures to reduce net sales growth by approximately 4&nbsp;percent; foreign currency exchange rates to reduce adjusted
operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth by approximately 1&nbsp;percent; and restructuring charges and project-related costs, transaction and acquisition integration costs related to actions previously announced, and product disposal
charges related to the ice cream recall to total approximately $45&nbsp;million to $50&nbsp;million. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net divestitures gain primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Please see
Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Transaction
costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax recovery</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs primarily resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2023. Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of
Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2023. Valuation adjustments of certain corporate
investments in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 5. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges (recoveries</U>) </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Voluntary
recall costs recorded in fiscal 2023 related to certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products. Please see Note 5. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth on a Constant-currency Basis </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our
